 Nadisutra: Ekasukha
 is shabd se shushk or daraar se fatty jameen or upar chilchilaataa meghaviheen aasmaan dimag main kaundhta he
 When the rains get dirty, the river drains, village wells all dry up
 khet dhul se bhare katoron main badal jate hai
 Animals and birds wander thirsty
 yah kaali chaaya in garmiyon main hakeekat ban gai he or isane pehle hi chintajanak shakl akhriyaar kar lee he

 aise main yaad aata he ki hamaari sadanira nadiyon kaa kya hua? nadisutra shrinkhalaa us sutara ko talashne kii koshish he jise hamane bhula diya he
 After all, the country which developed its cities on the banks of rivers, the country which developed its rituals of worship along the rivers and rivers, the rivers were considered to be goddesses, how did this sutra disappear? aakhir, hamaare sabase puraane granth, jo devon kii vaani bhi he, rugveda samet tamaam vedon, upanishdon, brahmanon main nadiyon or uski mahima kaa vistaar se zikr he
 It is said in the seventeenth Sukta of the Dasam Mandal of the Rigveda: Ganges in me! Yamuna! Saraswati! Shatudri! Stomach true purity
 asiktya marud vrudhe! vitastya jikaye! shrrinuhyasuvaiyaya
 
 to achaanak hamaare samaaj ko kya ho gaya ki hamane nadiyon or jhil-talabon ko koodaydaan samaj liya? unhen sukha dene kii sajeesh karne lage
 Along every river in our country there are folk songs, folklore associated with them
 thodaa itihaas bhi he or thodaa vigyaan bhi
 Tradition and customs are good anyway
 aise main nadiyon ko lekar ham kya sochate hai, nadisutra uskaa ek kism kaa yah reality check bhi he
 i myself have traveled from Gomukh to Gangasagar on the banks of the Ganges
 desh kaise nadiyon ko bhul gaya he or apni nadiyon kii sthiti paristhiti unki katha or vyathaa ko shrinkhalabaddh tareeke se pesh karne kii koshish karuunga
 It is expected that the society standing, raising and growing along the banks of the rivers will remember its reservoirs, ponds, puddles, ponds, stepwells and rivulets
 is shrinkhalaa main koshish yah hogi isamen padhane waalon ko sirf nakaaratmakataa or hataasha bhare byore hi na milen
 Not only the Ganges, all the rivers along the banks of the country, as far as i have traveled, from whom i have met, all the talk of them, their batras, their stories and their folk songs and folklore is not a huge, but a unique and We have experienced a new type, and will try to put it in front of you
 safar main hamen kai vaigyanik mili, inamen se kai ganga nadi kii anokhi swayanshuddhi kshamta par baat karte rahe
 Not only the Ganges, there were many people who talked about the pollution of all the rivers, many devotees met who only kept talking about mythology and reverence
 jinke liye ganga-yamuna-narmada-kaveri-godavari agaadh aasthaa kaa strot hai
 But we found many people who told us stories related to rivers in the lobby of a tea shop or a hotel
 inamen se kuch kahaniyaan puranic hai, kuch kinvadantiyaan or dantakathaayen hai to kuch lokkathaayen
 Many of these storytellers were from different regions, who were telling us stories of their area far from their roots, in which there was some river or other
 inamen hotel manager se waiter tak, nadiyon main chappu chalaane vaale navik se lekar pandit tak or kapade saaf kar rahe dhobi se lekar chaay kii dukaan par baithe gapod tak sab hai

 vah raipur se aae the
 To visit Mata Vindhyavasini
 unhone bhojali kaa geet sunaaya tha

 lekin kai vidwaanon ne ganga kii haalat ke liye bhrashtachar or raajnneetik agenda main nadiyon ke na hone ke alaava ek nayaa tathy bhi saamne rakhaa

 yani hamaare desh main nadiyon ko lekar tathakthith visheshgyon kii dakshata or vichaar

 yani, badi pariyojnaayen bananaa or lagu karnaa

 hamen nadiyon ko saath rakhkar aage badhanaa siikhnaa hoga

 The flood and devastation in Kedarnath has completed two years but the Central Government has not been able to answer a question of the Supreme Court till now
 yah ek aisa sawaal he jo tay karegaa ki himalay main vikaas kii disha kya hogi or vahaan tarakkee kaa kya model apanaaya jaayegaa
 In June 2013, the Himalayas witnessed the biggest disaster of its history
 kedarnath main ai baadh main hazaron logon kii jaan gai
 The official death toll is around six thousand, but it is known that far more people died in Uttarakhand
 kai ghar tabah huye or karodon kii sampatti bah gai
 Two years later, many questions remain to be answered
 intazaar supreme court kii ore se kiye gayi us sawaal ke jawaab kaa bhi he jisamen adaalat ne sarkaar se poocha ki kedarnath traasadee main uttarakhand main ban rahe baandhon kaa kya role he? do saal baad ab bhi sarkaar is sawaal kaa jawaab taal rahi he
 On June 3 this month, the Central Government issued a new order and formed a new committee
 yah cameti kedarnath traasadee par ab tak di gai sari report ko rivyuu karegi
 The government had said in court that it would once again include some experts in the committee and submit its report on the impact of dams in the Himalayan region of Uttarakhand
 lekin sarkaar ne pehle banaai gai ravi chopra cameti ke ek sadsy ko chhodkar saare sadsy badal diye hai
 The Central Government is saying that the appointment of the panel has been done under the rules and according to the order of the court, but the people fighting for the environment of rivers and Himalayas are not happy with this decision
 baandhon, nadiyon or insaani zindagi par unke asar kaa lambey samay se adhyayan kar rahe himanshu thakkar kehete hai, ‚Äòcentre sarkaar or uttarakhand sarkaar uttarakhand ke logon kii zindagi or ganga ke astitv ke saath khilwaad kar rahi he
 The Supreme Court is being misled by giving importance to the profits of some dam companies
 sarkaar ne ek taraf pehle halafanama dekar kaha ki baandhon kaa aapadaa main haath tha
 Then assured the court that she would include some information in the old committee and review the reports so far
 lekin ab jo nai cameti bani he usamen koi swatantra log nahin hai
